{{Use mdy dates|date=January 2020}}
[[File:Nintendo 3DS case banners.png|300px|thumb|right|The international white Nintendo 3DS banner used on current and upcoming retail game covers (top). In Japan, the banner is black for Nintendo 3DS games rated by [[Computer Entertainment Rating Organization|CERO]] as C or higher (bottom). [[List of Nintendo Network games#Nintendo 3DS|Nintendo Network-compatible games]] feature a small logo on top of the banner, but as of November 2014, the small [[Amiibo]] logo is dominantly featured instead, even if said games also supported Nintendo Network. The Nintendo Network logo will continue to feature if Amiibo support is definitely absent. Actual retail game case covers the banner are flipped vertically. Game cases for games dedicated exclusively to [[New Nintendo 3DS]] (such as ''[[Xenoblade Chronicles 3D]]'') feature a different template layout.]]

This is a '''list of [[Nintendo 3DS]] games''' released or planned for release physically on [[Nintendo 3DS#Game card|Nintendo 3DS game cards]] and/or digitally on the [[Nintendo eShop]].

== Games ==
The Nintendo 3DS portable system has a library of games, which are released in game card and/or digital form.<ref>{{cite web|url=http://www.eurogamer.net/articles/nintendo-3ds-tech-specifications|title=Nintendo 3DS tech specifications|website=Eurogamer|accessdate=June 16, 2010}}</ref> Numerous titles of games here are subject to change. This list does not include downloadable games available via the [[Virtual Console]] service.<ref>{{cite web|url=http://ds.ign.com/articles/112/1124157p1.html|title=3DS Getting Its Own Virtual Console Store|website=IGN|accessdate=January 6, 2011}}</ref> The [[Nintendo 3DS family]] is [[backward compatible]] with its predecessor, the [[Nintendo DS line]], and [[List of Nintendo DS games|its software]], including most [[List of DSiWare games and applications|DSi software]].<ref>{{cite press release|url=https://www.nintendo.co.jp/ir/pdf/2010/100323e.pdf|title=Launch of New Portable Game Machine|website=Nintendo of Japan|accessdate=March 23, 2010|location=Minami-ku, Kyoto}}</ref>
The list is initially organized alphabetically by their English titles or their alphabet conversions, but it is also possible to sort each column individually by clicking the square icon at the top of each column. The Nintendo 3DS system is region locked, meaning that in reality each system has a restricted library of games to select from, depending on the region of the device;<ref>{{cite web|title=3DS region block confirmed, US won't even read JP games|url=http://www.destructoid.com/3ds-region-block-confirmed-us-won-t-even-read-jp-games-197176.phtml|website=Destructoid|accessdate=November 10, 2013}}</ref> the list below displays the availability of games within each of the four regions.

For a chronological list, click the sort button in any of the available regions' column. Games dated February 26, 2011, (Japan), March 25, 2011, (Europe), March 27, 2011, (North America), and March 31, 2011, (Australia) are the launch titles of each respective region.

There are '''{{table row counter|id=softwarelist|ignore=3}}'''{{efn|This number is always up to date by this [[Template:Table row counter|script]].}} games on this list.
